Accessibility digest

PageMeridian Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.meridiansenior.com/senior-living/nd/minot/the-wellington/contact-us
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score1207
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1207, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 279. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 26. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 101

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 63 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 2 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 73 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 76

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 48 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 17 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 4 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 16 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R37, score 1 (Text has less than the minimum contrast)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 27 (Very low contrast)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 71

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 12 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 64 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 56

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 33 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 9 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 36 (Text has insufficient contrast)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R76, score 1 (Text has less than the enhanced minimum contrast)
  • Package tenon, test 95, score 1 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
